\begin{isamarkuptext}%
The following is a helper function to connect the gas monad with the state monad.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isacommand{fun}\isamarkupfalse%
\isanewline
\ \ toState\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}State\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a{\isacharcomma}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}e{\isacharcomma}{\kern0pt}\ Gas{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ state{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}monad{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}a{\isacharcomma}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}e{\isacharcomma}{\kern0pt}\ State{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ state{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}monad{\isachardoublequoteclose}\ \isakeyword{where}\isanewline
\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}toState\ gm\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}{\isasymlambda}s{\isachardot}{\kern0pt}\ case\ gm\ s\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}gas\ s{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ of\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Normal\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}a{\isacharcomma}{\kern0pt}g{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ Normal{\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}a{\isacharcomma}{\kern0pt}s{\isasymlparr}gas{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}g{\isasymrparr}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ {\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ Exception\ e\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ Exception\ e{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\isanewline
\isacommand{lemma}\isamarkupfalse%
\ wptoState{\isacharbrackleft}{\kern0pt}wprule{\isacharbrackright}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \isakeyword{assumes}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isasymAnd}a\ g{\isachardot}{\kern0pt}\ gm\ s\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}gas\ s{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ Normal\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}a{\isacharcomma}{\kern0pt}\ g{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymLongrightarrow}\ P\ a\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}s{\isasymlparr}gas{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}g{\isasymrparr}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isasymAnd}e{\isachardot}{\kern0pt}\ gm\ s\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}gas\ s{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ Exception\ e\ {\isasymLongrightarrow}\ E\ e{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \isakeyword{shows}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}wp\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}toState\ gm{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ P\ E\ s{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline

\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Now we define the semantics of statements.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isacommand{function}\isamarkupfalse%
\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}domintros{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ stmt\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}S\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ Environment\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ CalldataT\ {\isasymRightarrow}\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}unit{\isacharcomma}{\kern0pt}\ Ex{\isacharcomma}{\kern0pt}\ State{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ state{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}monad{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ \isakeyword{where}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}stmt\ SKIP\ e\ cd\ st\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}do\ {\isacharbraceleft}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \ \ assert\ Gas\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}{\isasymlambda}st{\isachardot}{\kern0pt}\ gas\ st\ {\isachargreater}{\kern0pt}\ costs\ SKIP\ e\ cd\ st{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isacharsemicolon}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \ \ modify\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}{\isasymlambda}st{\isachardot}{\kern0pt}\ st{\isasymlparr}gas\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ gas\ st\ {\isacharminus}{\kern0pt}\ costs\ SKIP\ e\ cd\ st{\isasymrparr}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ {\isacharbraceright}{\kern0pt}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ st{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
{\isacharbar}{\kern0pt}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}stmt\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}ASSIGN\ lv\ ex{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ env\ cd\ st\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
